<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поинтересоваться.html>поинтересова́ться</a> (2369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересовать.html>интересова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">interesovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поинтересоваться.html>поинтересова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pointeresovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересоваться.html>интересова́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be curious</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ин<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***поискавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поискавший.html>поиска́вший</a> (4330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поискавший.html>поиска́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poiskávšij</span>)
</p>

***поить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поить.html>пои́ть</a> (6302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">поити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pojìti</i>. Derived from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pojь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">drink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поить.html>пои́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напоить.html>напои́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to water, to give to drink</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>и́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:напоить.html>напои́ть</a>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойло.html>по́йло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pójlo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойло.html>по́йла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойло.html>по́йла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойло.html>по́йл</a></b>)

***поймать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поймать.html>пойма́ть</a> (1380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поймать.html>пойма́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pojmátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поймать.html>пойма́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тачка.html>та́чку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pojmátʹ</b> táčku</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to catch</b> a taxi</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>по́й</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-йм-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.  | Кузнецова, Ефремова, 1986 |

***пойти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойти́</a> (165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-йти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pojtí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a></b>) <i>(concrete verbs)</i>
</p>
<ol><li>to go
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойди́те</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мной</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Pojdíte</b> so mnoj.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Come</b> with me. (polite)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to walk</li>
<li>to rain</li>
<li>to function, to work</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>Идти́</a></b> and <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойти́</a></a> are Russian concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a>, is an abstract verb.
</p>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>по́й</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,   <a href = vnd.unilang:изолированный.html>изоли́рованное</a> спряжение, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — ^b/b(9).     <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существовать.html>существу́ет</a> устар. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> деепричастия <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> <i>поше́д</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:употреблявшийся.html>употребля́вшаяся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:преимущественно.html>преиму́щественно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> XIX <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>ве́ке</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a>.

***пока.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a> (150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poká</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>for the present, for the time being
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poká</b> što</i> ― <span class="e-translation">meanwhile, in the meantime</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лаю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja <b>poká</b> što éto sdélaju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’ll do it in the meanwhile.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>for now <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">at the moment; until later</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poká</b> vsjó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">that’s all; that will do</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посмотреть.html>посмо́трим</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Poká</b> xvátit, a závtra posmótrim</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Тhat's enough for now and let's see (again) tomorrow.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poká</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>so long as, while
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рство</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ды</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рства</a>. (влади́мир ле́нин)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Poká</b> jestʹ gosudárstvo, net svobódy. Kogdá búdet svobóda, ne búdet gosudárstva. (Vladímir Lénin)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>While</b> the State exists, there can be no freedom. When there is freedom there will be no State. (Vladimir Lenin)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The subordinate clause that has <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a></b> must have an imperfective verb. The main clause could either have an imperfective or a perfective verb.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poká ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покамест.html>пока́мест</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pokámest</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poká</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bye; so long; I’ll see you later; see you soon.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:показатель.html>показа́тель</a> (4992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показать.html>показа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokazátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to show, to point</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">er</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показатель.html>показа́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokazátelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показатель.html>показа́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показатель.html>показа́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показатель.html>показа́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">показа́тельница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>indicator, measure, index <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">sign, indication, token</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>exponent, index</li>
<li>figure</li>
<li>rate, ratio</li>
<li>parameter, factor</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:показательный.html>показа́тельный</a> (9064)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показатель.html>показа́тель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokazátelʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">index, indicator, exponent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показательный.html>показа́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokazátelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>significant, revealing, indicative</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> demonstration
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показательный.html>показа́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>су́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pokazátelʹnyj súd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">show trial</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> model</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> exponential</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тель<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>показа́тельнее, показа́тельней.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-показ-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-тельн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:показать.html>показа́ть</a> (350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показать.html>показа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показывать.html>пока́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show</li>
<li>to display, to reveal, to achieve</li>
<li>to register, to read <i>(of measuring devices)</i></li>
<li>to point</li>
<li>to depose, to testify, to give evidence</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:показаться.html>показа́ться</a> (466)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показать.html>показа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показаться.html>показа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokazátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>каза́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показываться.html>пока́зываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to appear, to come into view, to come in sight</li>
<li>to turn up, to show up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seem</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показать.html>показа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показной.html>показно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokaznój</span>)

<li>ostensible</li>
<li>affected</li>
<li>vain</li>
<li>tinsel, theatrical</li></ol>

***показуха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:показуха.html>показу́ха</a> (22841)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показуха.html>показу́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokazúxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показуха.html>показу́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показуха.html>показу́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показуха.html>показу́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> disapprovingly</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> window-dressing, ostentation, pretense, (fake) show, veneer, facade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сплошной.html>сплошна́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:показуха.html>показу́ха</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto splošnája <b>pokazúxa</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it's all put on, just for show</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:показуха.html>показу́хи</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dlja <b>pokazúxi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">just for show</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***показывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:показывать.html>пока́зывать</a> (700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показать.html>показа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показывать.html>пока́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показать.html>показа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show</li>
<li>to display, to reveal</li>
<li>to achieve <i>(some result)</i></li>
<li>to show, to register, to read</li>
<li>to point <i>(at)</i></li>
<li>to depose, to testify, to give evidence</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показывать.html>пока́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показываться.html>пока́зываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokázyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показаться.html>показа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show oneself, to come in sight, to appear</li>
<li>to show up, to appear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:показываться.html>пока́зываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokázyvatʹsja</b> na glazá komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to appear in someone's presence</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:показываться.html>пока́зываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:врач.html>врачу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokázyvatʹsja</b> vračú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to see a doctor</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показывать.html>пока́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***покалечить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покалечить.html>покале́чить</a> (15603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калечить.html>кале́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kaléčitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to maim, cripple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покалечить.html>покале́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokaléčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калечить.html>кале́чить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cripple, to maim, to mutilate</li>
<li>to pervert, to twist, to warp</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кале́чение</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kaléčenije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ле́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чить</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:калечить.html>кале́чить</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-калеч-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***покаравший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покарать.html>покара́вший</a> (19813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покарать.html>покара́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokarávšij</span>)
